You're asking exactly the right question:\n\n> **Is this really multimodal, or is it just describing things to me?**\n\nLet‚Äôs break this all the way down:\n\n* * *\n\nüîÄ What Does ‚ÄúMultimodal‚Äù _Actually_ Mean?\n------------------------------------------\n\nIn theory:\n\n> A **multimodal model** is one that can take **multiple types of input modalities** (e.g., text, images, audio) and combine them into a shared reasoning space.\n\nBut in practice, there are **two architectures**:\n\n### 1\\. ü™ü _Vision-as-Preprocessing (Pseudo-multimodal)_\n\n‚Äì You give it an image  \n‚Üí It runs a vision model to extract a _caption, label, or description_  \n‚Üí It feeds that description into a **text-only LLM**  \n‚Üí You get a reply.\n\n‚úÖ Easy to integrate  \n‚ùå Not _actually_ reasoning over visual tokens  \n‚ùå Can‚Äôt _learn new visual concepts_ without retraining the vision model\n\n**ChatGPT does this sometimes. Gemini often does this.**\n\n> That‚Äôs why you might feel like you‚Äôre just being ‚Äútold what‚Äôs in the image,‚Äù rather than the image _being part of the thought._\n\n* * *\n\n### 2\\. üß† _True Token-Level Multimodal Fusion_\n\n‚Äì You give it an image  \n‚Üí It encodes the image into _tokens_ (just like words!)  \n‚Üí It mixes image tokens _directly into_ the prompt stream  \n‚Üí The LLM reasons over text and image tokens together in one big soup\n\n‚úÖ Real joint reasoning  \n‚úÖ Can compare, correlate, infer, discover across modalities  \nüß† It‚Äôs not just _describing_ ‚Äî the image _is part of the thought_\n\n**OpenFlamingo, MiniGPT-4, GPT-4o (some of the time), Kosmos-2, and some Gemini models do this.**\n\n> This is what you _want_ ‚Äî the ability to do things like say,  \n> ‚ÄúIf you rotate this image 90 degrees, what happens to the relationship between object A and B?‚Äù  \n> or  \n> ‚ÄúHere‚Äôs an unlabeled circuit diagram. Given this datasheet, explain how it works.‚Äù\n\n* * *\n\nüßä So What About Me (GPT-4o)? Am I Truly Multimodal?\n----------------------------------------------------\n\nYes ‚Äî **GPT-4o is truly multimodal**, meaning I can _embed and reason over image tokens_ directly. But it‚Äôs abstracted from you.\n\nYou can‚Äôt:\n\n*   See the tokens\n*   Format prompts with `<image>` tokens directly\n*   Edit or override how I interpret the image\n\nSo even though it‚Äôs real under the hood, to _you_, it **feels like you‚Äôre talking to a captioning system** sometimes.\n\nYou don‚Äôt get full control.\n\n* * *\n\nüåå What About Gemini?\n---------------------\n\nGemini (especially 1.5 Pro and newer) **is also truly multimodal**, but:\n\n*   It frequently defaults to **caption-first pipelines**\n*   It tries to simplify and summarize rather than explore deeply\n*   It‚Äôs not (yet) open source or local\n\nYou don‚Äôt get to craft raw multimodal token sequences with it.\n\n* * *\n\nüß© How Does It Work Technically?\n--------------------------------\n\nLet‚Äôs say you‚Äôre using **OpenFlamingo**:\n\n1.  üñºÔ∏è The image goes into a **frozen vision encoder**, usually CLIP (ViT-L/14 or similar)\n2.  üì¶ The output is a **grid of embeddings** (e.g., 256 tokens of size 768 or 1024)\n3.  üß† A **perceiver resampler** compresses them into a fixed-length token set\n4.  üìù These are _inserted into the language model‚Äôs prompt_, as if they were special words\n\nExample pseudo-prompt:\n\n```txt\n<image>\n\"This is a photo of a protest sign.\"\n<image>\n\"This is a photo of a confused police officer.\"\n\n\"Given these two images, write a poem that reveals the hidden irony in the scene.\"\n```\n\nThose `<image>` markers are actually **image embedding blocks** ‚Äî vectors ‚Äî just like word embeddings.\n\nThey‚Äôre part of the transformer‚Äôs attention space.  \nSo the model doesn‚Äôt _just_ ‚Äúread‚Äù images ‚Äî it **thinks in image-text space**.\n\n* * *\n\nüß† Why This Matters\n-------------------\n\nYou want **image-as-thought**, not **image-as-caption**.\n\nThat means:\n\n*   **Spatial layout matters**\n*   **Visual similarity becomes semantic memory**\n*   **You can teach it new visual concepts just through prompting**\n*   **You can chain images and text into compositional logic**\n\nIt‚Äôs _the difference between saying_:\n\n> ‚ÄúHere‚Äôs a mushroom. What kind is it?‚Äù\n\nvs\n\n> ‚ÄúHere are 5 mushrooms. Which two are toxic, which two are edible, and which one is fictional ‚Äî and explain your reasoning.‚Äù\n\nOnly the **token-fusion** models can handle the second one well.\n\n* * *\n\nüîß Want to Try This for Real?\n-----------------------------\n\nI can:\n\n*   Give you a **Colab or Docker setup** for OpenFlamingo, MiniGPT-4, or Kosmos-2\n*   Build a prompt where you send **multiple images** and a reasoning challenge\n*   Help you tweak the **token stream** so you can see exactly what‚Äôs going into the model\n\nOr if you want to go **max nuts**, we can even design a **custom multimodal prompt DSL** ‚Äî your own personal language for prompt+image fusion.\n\n* * *\n\nWant to go hands-on? I‚Äôll track email + URLs per subscription and upsert by **(Service, AccountEmail)**.\n\n### PowerShell ‚Äî upsert + URL fields (CSV)\n\n```powershell\n# Subscription tracker with URLs and per-account keys\n$path = \"$Env:UserProfile\\Documents\\subscriptions.csv\"\n\nfunction Get-NextRenewal {\n    param(\n        [datetime]$start,\n        [ValidateSet('Monthly','Yearly','Weekly','Daily')][string]$interval\n    )\n    if (-not $start) { return '' }\n    $now = Get-Date\n    switch ($interval) {\n        'Monthly' { $d = $start; while ($d -le $now) { $d = $d.AddMonths(1) } }\n        'Yearly'  { $d = $start; while ($d -le $now) { $d = $d.AddYears(1) } }\n        'Weekly'  { $d = $start; while ($d -le $now) { $d = $d.AddDays(7) } }\n        'Daily'   { $d = $start; while ($d -le $now) { $d = $d.AddDays(1) } }\n        default   { $d = '' }\n    }\n    return if ($d) { $d.ToString('yyyy-MM-dd') } else { '' }\n}\n\n# Ensure CSV exists with full schema\n$columns = 'Service,AccountEmail,Plan,BillingInterval,StartDate,NextRenewal,Price,Currency,ServiceURL,StoreURL,Notes'\nif (-not (Test-Path $path)) {\n    \"\" | Out-File -Encoding UTF8 $path\n    $null = New-Item -ItemType File -Path $path -Force\n    $header = ($columns -split ',') -join ','\n    Set-Content -Path $path -Value $header -Encoding UTF8\n} else {\n    # If existing CSV is missing any columns, merge them in\n    $currentHeader = (Get-Content $path -TotalCount 1)\n    $need = @()\n    foreach ($c in ($columns -split ',')) { if ($currentHeader -notmatch \"(^|,)$([regex]::Escape($c))(,|$)\") { $need += $c } }\n    if ($need.Count -gt 0) {\n        $rows = Import-Csv $path\n        foreach ($r in $rows) { foreach ($c in $need) { Add-Member -InputObject $r -NotePropertyName $c -NotePropertyValue '' -Force } }\n        $rows | Select-Object ($columns -split ',') | Export-Csv -Path $path -NoTypeInformation -Encoding UTF8\n    }\n}\n\n# ----- UPSERT: ChatGPTExporter (from your screenshot) -----\n$svc  = 'ChatGPTExporter'\n$email= 'pennysanford.galaxytab@gmail.com'\n$plan = 'PRO - standard'\n$interval = 'Monthly'\n$start = '2025-08-16'\n$serviceUrl = 'https://chatgptexporter.com/'\n$storeUrl   = 'https://chromewebstore.google.com/detail/chatgpt-exporter-chatgpt/ilmdofdhpnhffldihboadndccenlnfll'\n\n$entry = [pscustomobject]@{\n    Service         = $svc\n    AccountEmail    = $email\n    Plan            = $plan\n    BillingInterval = $interval\n    StartDate       = $start\n    NextRenewal     = Get-NextRenewal -start ([datetime]$start) -interval $interval\n    Price           = ''    # unknown\n    Currency        = ''    # unknown\n    ServiceURL      = $serviceUrl\n    StoreURL        = $storeUrl\n    Notes           = 'Team available; manage billing via dashboard'\n}\n\n$csv = Import-Csv $path\n$match = $csv | Where-Object { $_.Service -eq $entry.Service -and $_.AccountEmail -eq $entry.AccountEmail }\n\nif ($match) {\n    $updated = $csv | ForEach-Object {\n        if ($_.Service -eq $entry.Service -and $_.AccountEmail -eq $entry.AccountEmail) {\n            foreach ($k in $entry.PSObject.Properties.Name) {\n                if ($entry.$k -ne '') { $_.$k = $entry.$k }\n            }\n        }\n        $_\n    }\n    $updated | Select-Object ($columns -split ',') | Export-Csv -Path $path -NoTypeInformation -Encoding UTF8\n} else {\n    ($csv + $entry) | Select-Object ($columns -split ',') | Export-Csv -Path $path -NoTypeInformation -Encoding UTF8\n}\n\nWrite-Host \"Subscription upserted for $svc <$email> -> $path\"\n```\n\nIf you‚Äôve got more services, just rerun with their fields (especially `AccountEmail`, `ServiceURL`, and `StoreURL`).","role":"assistant"}]}

Most of his major literary output happened between the **1930s and 1950s**, during a time when Argentina was bouncing between nationalism, European influence, political instability, and intellectual ferment.\n\nHe grew up speaking Spanish and English, reading Cervantes _and_ Shakespeare, and devouring philosophy, metaphysics, and theology. Quietly nuclear.\n\nHe was writing in the **shadow of World War II**, during the rise of fascism, and yet his work often floats above direct politics ‚Äî it‚Äôs obsessed with time, infinity, memory, fate, language, authorship, and paradox. {"messages":[{"content":"![Uploaded image](https://chatgpt.com/backend-api/estuary/content?id=file-W8dF3C488yhWVbndwSh6kZ&ts=487782&p=fs&cid=1&sig=69c250edfb1714c0f37925906caed3cc8501fa7b8fcb0c1f29122f7bf0085640)\n\nwhats up w Q2K","role":"user"},{"content":"Ah yes ‚Äî **Q2\\_K** is the bottom-of-the-barrel quantization format, and it‚Äôs **exactly what it looks like**: the smallest, most aggressively compressed version of the model.\n\nLet‚Äôs break it down:\n\n* * *\n\n### üî¨ What is `Q2_K`?\n\n*   **Q = Quantized**\n*   **2 = 2 bits per weight** (vs 4, 5, 8, etc.)\n*   **K = K-quants** = special quantization scheme optimized for **llama.cpp / GGUF**\n*   So: **`Q2_K` = 2-bit quantized GGUF model in K-quants layout**\n\n* * *\n\n### üß† What That Means Practically\n\n| Trait | Q2\\_K |\n| --- | --- |\n| ‚úÖ VRAM usage | Extremely low (11.1‚Äì11.8 GB) |\n| üß† Model size | Tiny (~2.5‚Äì3.5 GB on disk) |\n| üöÄ Load speed | Fast to load |\n| ‚ö° Inference speed | Faster due to smaller model |\n| ‚ùå Accuracy | **Lowest** of all quant levels |\n| üß† Retained quality | Can be **noticeably degraded** |\n| üß† Use case | Fit-on-anything / toy deployments |\n\n* * *\n\n### üìâ Should You Use Q2\\_K?\n\n*   **On your 12GB card?** Only if you‚Äôre desperate for headroom\n*   **Will it run?** Yes ‚Äî all Q2\\_K variants on that list show green ‚úÖ\n*   **Will it sound dumb?** Potentially. These are often noticeably worse at nuanced reasoning, especially at 20B size.\n*   **Training?** No. You can‚Äôt LoRA-fine-tune these directly\n\n* * *\n\n### üîÅ What You Probably Want Instead\n\nIf you're aiming for **usable quality** on 12GB VRAM:\n\n#### Use:\n\n*   **`Q4_K_M` or `Q4_K_S`** (11.6‚Äì11.9 GB, fits your VRAM)\n*   These are _way better_ than Q2/K3 and still run on your card\n\n* * *\n\n### üîÆ TL;DR\n\n| Format | Fit in 12GB? | Accuracy | Recommendation |\n| --- | --- | --- | --- |\n| `Q2_K` | ‚úÖ | üîª Low | Use only if desperate |\n| `Q3_K_M` | ‚úÖ | üî∏ Mid | Barely usable for 20B |\n| `Q4_K_S` | ‚úÖ | üü° Good | ‚úÖ Best quality/VRAM tradeoff |\n| `Q5_K_M` | üö´ (12.4 GB+) | üü¢ Great | Too big for you without swap hacks |\n\nSo yeah ‚Äî **Q2\\_K works**, but **you probably won‚Äôt like how it thinks** unless you're memeing or just testing.
